					clamp_variable = {
						var = KIS_plebiscite_viridian_coast_support_var
						min = 0
						max = 1
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { 
						var = KIS_plebiscite_apricot_glen_support_var
						value = 0.1
					}
					clamp_variable = {
						var = KIS_plebiscite_apricot_glen_support_var
						min = 0
						max = 1
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { 
						var = KIS_plebiscite_verdant_fields_support_var
						value = 0.1
					}
					clamp_variable = {
						var = KIS_plebiscite_verdant_fields_support_var
						min = 0
						max = 1
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = KIR
							original_tag = KIC
							original_tag = KIS
						}
					}
					clr_country_flag = KIR_plebiscite_rain_shine_tour_started_flag
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIR_plebiscite_rain_shine_tour"
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = KIR
						original_tag = KIC
						original_tag = KIS
					}
				}
				news_event = { id = kirin_news.7 hours = 24 }
				set_country_flag = { flag = KIR_plebiscite_rain_shine_tour_started_flag value = 1 days = 70 }
			}
		}
	}
}

KIR_nakp_treasury_category = {
	KIR_nakp_treasury_monthly_income = {
		icon = gre_paying_ifc_debt
		allowed = { original_tag = KIS }
		activation = { always = no }
		available = { 
			hidden_trigger = { 
				always = no 
			}
		}
		
		fixed_random_seed = no
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		is_good = yes
		
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout KIR_nakp_treasury_monthly_income"
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFC value = KIS.num_of_civilian_factories }
			multiply_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFC value = KISTreasuryIncomePerFC }
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFM value = KIS.num_of_military_factories }
			multiply_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFM value = KISTreasuryIncomePerFM }
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFD value = KIS.num_of_naval_factories }
			multiply_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFD value = KISTreasuryIncomePerFD }
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = 0 }
			add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeFC }
			add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeFM }
			add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeFD }
			##############
			## Land Tax ##
			##############
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_state_land_tax_flag
				}
				set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeLandTax value = KIS.num_owned_controlled_states }
				multiply_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeLandTax value = 200 }
				add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = TreasuryIncomeLandTax }
			}
			###########
			## Tithe ##
			###########
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_corporate_tithes_flag
				}
				set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeTithe value = KIS.KIS_corporate_vassals_var }
				multiply_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeTithe value = 250 }
				add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = TreasuryIncomeTithe }
			}
			#############
			## Tourism ##
			#############
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_unlocked_tourism_flag
				}
				clear_variable = KIS_tourist_destinations_var
				clear_variable = KIS_tourist_destinations_income_var
				if = {
					limit = {
						909 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						924 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1054 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1097 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1132 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1135 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1139 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1158 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				set_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_income_var value = KIS_tourist_destinations_var }
				multiply_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_income_var value = 150 }
				add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KIS_tourist_destinations_income_var }
			}
			#############
			## SK-ENEZ ##
			#############
			if = {
				limit = {
					AUB = {
						exists = yes
						has_full_control_of_state = 833
						has_full_control_of_state = 1065
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = 4000 }
			}
			####################
			## Predict Income ##
			####################
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomePredicted value = TreasuryIncome }
			#########################################
			## A Little RNG -> "Accounting Errors" ##
			#########################################
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeMax value = TreasuryIncome }
			multiply_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeMax value = TreasuryAccountingError }
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeMin value = 0 }
			subtract_from_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeMin value = TreasuryIncomeMax }
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeRand value = 0 }
			randomize_variable = {
				var = TreasuryIncomeRand
				distribution = binomial
				min = ROOT.TreasuryIncomeMin
				max = ROOT.TreasuryIncomeMax
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = TreasuryIncomeRand }
			############################
			## Add Income to Treasury ##
			############################
			add_to_variable = { var = KIS.TreasuryWealth value = KIS.TreasuryIncome }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = KIS.TreasuryWealth
				min = 0
			}
			###################################################
			## Calculate Income Change from the Month Before ##
			###################################################
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow value = KIS.TreasuryIncome }
			if = {
				#########################################
				## If we made a Loss this (last) Month ##
				#########################################
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeMonthBefore > KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow } 
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { var = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow value = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeMonthBefore }
			}
			else = {
				subtract_from_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow value = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeMonthBefore }
			}
			set_variable = { var = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeChange value = KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow }
			round_variable = KISTreasuryIncomeChange
			#############################################
			## Set Income Change for this (last) Month ##
			#############################################
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeMonthBefore value = TreasuryIncome }
			##########################################
			## Add this Month's Income to the Array ##
			##########################################
			add_to_array = { array = KISTreasuryIncomeHistoryArray value = TreasuryIncome }
			#################################
			## Find Highest Income To Date ##
			#################################
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryHistoryHighestIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeHistoryArray^0 }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeHistoryArray
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { v > KISTreasuryHistoryHighestIncome }
					}
					set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryHistoryHighestIncome value = v }
				}
			}
			######################
			## Activate Mission ##
			######################
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_nakp_treasury_gain_monthly_income_tt
			activate_mission = KIR_nakp_treasury_monthly_income
		}
	}

		icon = generic_assassination
		allowed = {

		ai_will_do = {

			modifier = {

		custom_cost_text = KIS_buy_guns_GRI_cost_tt
		
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 30
		
		modifier = {
			political_power_factor = -0.05
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIS_buy_guns_GRI"
			if = {
				limit = {
					GRI = {
						has_tech = infantry_weapons
						NOT = {
							has_tech = infantry_weapons1
							has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_b
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_e
						}
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 2500 producer = GRI }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GRI = {
						has_tech = infantry_weapons1
						NOT = {
							has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_b
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_e
						}
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 2500 producer = GRI }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GRI = {
						has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
						NOT = {
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_b
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_e
						}
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_2 amount = 2500 producer = GRI }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GRI = {
						has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
						NOT = {
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_b
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_e
						}
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_3 amount = 2500 producer = GRI }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GRI = {
						has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_b
						NOT = {
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_e
						}
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_x amount = 2500 producer = GRI }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GRI = {
						has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons_e
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_x_2 amount = 2500 producer = GRI }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIS_buy_guns_GRI"
			hidden_effect = {

					var = TreasuryWealth
					value = KIS_buy_guns_GRI_cost

	KIS_demand_tribute = {
		icon = ger_mefo_bills
		allowed = {
			original_tag = KIS
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 25
		}
		
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = KIS_demand_tribute_unlocked_flag
		}
		
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = KIS
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			political_power_factor = 0.01
		}
		
		cost = 90
		days_remove = 90
		days_re_enable = 1005
		
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIS_demand_tribute"
			set_variable = { tribute_subject_num_states = FROM.num_owned_controlled_states }
			multiply_variable = { tribute_subject_num_states = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { KIS.TreasuryWealth = tribute_subject_num_states }
			clear_variable = tribute_subject_num_states
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIS_demand_tribute_add_wealth_tt
			FROM = {
				add_political_power = -25
				custom_effect_tooltip = KIS_demand_tribute_autonomy_score_add_50
				hidden_effect = {
					add_autonomy_score = {
						value = 50 
						localization = KIS_paid_tribute
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIS_demand_tribute"
		}
	}

		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_decision"
			if = { ##establishment-citizenry divide
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_establishment
					NOT = {	has_country_flag = KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_people }
				}
				add_to_variable = { KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_support_var = 0.15 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_establishment }
					has_country_flag = KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_people
				}
				randomize_temp_variable = {
					var = KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_support_var_PEOPLE_TEMP
					distribution = uniform
					min = 0.1
					max = 0.3
				}
				add_to_variable = { KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_support_var = KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_support_var_PEOPLE_TEMP }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_support_var = 0.05 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_decision_tt
			clamp_variable = {
				var = KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_support_var
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIS_plebiscite_rhapsody_decision"
			hidden_effect = {
				subtract_from_variable = { 
					var = TreasuryWealth
					value = 5000
				}
			}
		}

	KIS_zaikirian_commandery = {
		icon = generic_form_nation
		allowed = {
			original_tag = KIS
		}
		available = {
			has_government = fascism
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KIS_zaikirian_commandery_req_tt
				all_of_scopes = {
					array = KXN.core_states
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						PREV = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
					}
				}
				all_of_scopes = {
					array = NVA.core_states
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						PREV = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
					}
				}
				all_of_scopes = {
					array = KHM.core_states
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						PREV = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 70

		days_remove = 70

		fire_only_once = yes
		
		fixed_random_seed = no

        ai_will_do = {
			factor = 15
        }

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -0.15
		}
		
		#cosmetic_tag = KXN_KIR
		
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIS_zaikirian_commandery"
			hidden_effect = {
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = KIS
					save_event_target_as = KIS_zaikirian_commandery_target
					set_country_flag = KIS_zaikirian_commandery_flag
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_core_of = KZC
								is_core_of = KIS
							}
						}
						remove_core_of = KZC
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 0
						neutrality = 0
						fascism = 100
						communism = 0
					}
					KIS = { 
						KZC = { 
							transfer_technology = yes 
							transfer_society_ideas = yes
							transfer_science_ideas = yes
							transfer_poverty_ideas = yes
							transfer_illiteracy_ideas = yes
						} 
					}
					add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
					add_ideas = free_trade
					add_ideas = kirin_race
					add_ideas = limited_conscription
					add_ideas = KIR_jade_lotus_banner
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = fascism 
						long_name = KIRIN_VERMILION_PARTY_fascism_LONG
						name = KIRIN_VERMILION_PARTY_fascism
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = KXN_KIR
					load_focus_tree = blank_focus_tree
					set_rule = {
						can_create_factions = no
						can_boost_other_ideologies = no
						can_join_factions = no
						can_send_volunteers = no
						can_puppet = no
						can_lower_tension = no
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = KIS
						}
						event_target:KIS_zaikirian_commandery_target = {
							declare_war_on = {
								target = PREV
								type = topple_government
							}
						}
					}
					retire_ideology_leader = fascism
					retire_ideology_leader = communism
					retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
					retire_ideology_leader = democratic
					random_list = {
						1 = { 
							set_country_leader_portrait = {
							  portrait = "GFX_portrait_unknown_kirin_female"
							}
						}
						1 = { 
							set_country_leader_portrait = {
							  portrait = "GFX_portrait_unknown_kirin_male"
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_leader_ideology = falangism
				}
				puppet = KZC
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						OR = {

					add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
					add_ideas = free_trade
					add_ideas = kirin_race
					add_ideas = limited_conscription
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = fascism 
						long_name = KIRIN_VERMILION_PARTY_fascism_LONG
						name = KIRIN_VERMILION_PARTY_fascism
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = LMB_KIR
					load_focus_tree = blank_focus_tree
					set_rule = {
						can_create_factions = no
						can_boost_other_ideologies = no
						can_join_factions = no
						can_send_volunteers = no
						can_puppet = no
						can_lower_tension = no
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = KIS
						}
						event_target:KIS_LMB_viceroyalty_target = {
							declare_war_on = {
								target = PREV
								type = topple_government
							}
						}
					}
					retire_ideology_leader = fascism
					retire_ideology_leader = communism
					retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
					retire_ideology_leader = democratic
					random_list = {
						1 = { 
							set_country_leader_portrait = {
							  portrait = "GFX_portrait_unknown_kirin_female"
							}
						}
						1 = { 
							set_country_leader_portrait = {
							  portrait = "GFX_portrait_unknown_kirin_male"
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_leader_ideology = neofeudalism
				}
				puppet = KLV
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = KIS
							is_subject_of = KIS
						}
						PREV = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
					}
					is_core_of = LMB
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_core_of = KLV
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = KIS_LMB_viceroyalty_decision_state_ownership_tt
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = KLV.core_states
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								tag = KIS
								is_subject_of = KIS
							}
							PREV = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
						}
					}
					KLV = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				KLV = {
					set_capital = {
						state = 1099
					}
				}
			}
		}
    }

KIC_moving_capital_category = {
	KIC_move_capital_to_decision = {
		icon = SOV_place_hq
		allowed = {
			original_tag = KIC
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only

		visible = {
			FROM = {
				is_controlled_by = KIC
				NOT = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KIC_move_capital_to_decision_req_tt
				FROM = {
					any_neighbor_state = { 
						is_capital = yes
						is_controlled_by = KIC
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KIC_not_moving_capital_req_tt
				KIC = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = KIC_is_moving_capital_flag
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		state_target = yes
		target_array = KIC_move_capital_eligible_states_array

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 50
		}

		cost = 25
		days_remove = KIC.KIC_move_capital_duration_var

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain_mult = -0.05
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIC_move_capital_to_decision target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = KIC_is_moving_capital_flag
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIC_move_capital_to_decision target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = KIC_is_moving_capital_flag
				capital_scope = {
					remove_province_modifier = { 
						static_modifiers = { rising_sun_headquarters_core rising_sun_headquarters_non_core }
						province = {
							all_provinces = yes
						}
					}
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_core_state }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_non_core_state }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_core_state_REAL }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_non_core_state_REAL }
				}
			}
			set_capital = {
				state = FROM
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_core_of = KIC
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = KIC_move_capital_to_decision_core_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					FROM = {
						add_province_modifier = {
							static_modifiers = { rising_sun_headquarters_core }
							province = {
								all_provinces = yes
							}
						}
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_core_state }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_core_state_REAL }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = KIC
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = KIC_move_capital_to_decision_non_core_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					FROM = {
						add_province_modifier = {
							static_modifiers = { rising_sun_headquarters_non_core }
							province = {
								all_provinces = yes
							}
						}
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_non_core_state }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_non_core_state_REAL }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_controlled_by = KIC
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = KIC_is_moving_capital_flag
		}
	}

				}

					text = {

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 15
		}
		
		visible = {
			ROOT = {
				has_country_flag = CHN_FRV_flag
				has_country_flag = CFR_infiltrate_country_available
				has_country_flag = CFR_BBO_visible
			}
		}
		
		target_array = CFR_infiltrated_countries_array
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				check_variable = { CFR_black_bag_operation_var < 4 }
			}
		}
		
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 14
			has_political_power > 14
		}
		
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_CP_15_pp_15
		
		modifier = {
			command_power_gain_mult = 0.02
		}
		
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 60
		
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision CFR_black_bag_operation"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = -15
				add_command_power = -15
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove CFR_black_bag_operation"
			FROM = {
				add_to_variable = { CFR_black_bag_operation_var = 1 } 
				save_current_manpower = yes 
				capital_scope = { add_manpower = -100 }
				restore_previous_manpower = yes 
			}
			add_relation_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = CFR_black_bag_operation_modifier
			}
		}
	}

				add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -1 }
				country_event = { id = kirin_utility.33 days = 365 }
			}
		}

		}

			}
		}

	CFR_resource_operation = {
		icon = steel
		allowed = {
			original_tag = CHN
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 15
		}
		
		visible = {
			ROOT = {
				has_country_flag = CHN_FRV_flag
				has_country_flag = CFR_infiltrate_country_state_available
				has_country_flag = CFR_resource_operation_visible
			}
		}
		
		state_target = yes
		on_map_mode = map_only
		target_array = CFR_infiltrated_countries_states_array
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_owned_by = CFR
					is_controlled_by = CFR
					has_state_flag = CFR_stole_resources_from_this_state
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = FROM.resource@crystals
						value = 1
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FROM.resource@chromium
						value = 1
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FROM.resource@steel
						value = 1
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FROM.resource@tungsten
						value = 1
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FROM.resource@rubber
						value = 1
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FROM.resource@aluminium
						value = 1
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FROM.resource@oil
						value = 1
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			check_variable = { ROOT.infiltrators_var > 4 }
			command_power > 14
		}
		
		custom_cost_text = CFR_steal_factories_cost
		
		modifier = {
		}
		
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 80
		
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision CFR_resource_operation"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -15
				subtract_from_variable = { ROOT.infiltrators_var = 5 }
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove CFR_resource_operation"
			FROM.owner = {
				give_resource_rights = { receiver = CFR state = FROM }
				custom_effect_tooltip = CFR_resource_operation_tt
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					set_state_flag = CFR_stole_resources_from_this_state
					state_event = {
						id = kirin_utility.35
						days = 365
						trigger_for = controller
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
